For lunch, we tried out Eat 24 and decided to get food from Elixiria. At first, I was kind of iffy about it because when I was scrolling through the menu, it was different. Way different from what I'm used to ordering. My first thought was "wow, it's healthy here."

After looking around, I decided to order the Honey Mustard Atlantic Salmon. Unfortunately, the wait was more than an hour and a half to go, so that was a huge buzz kill.

When it finally arrived, it was a bit cold. I don't know if it was supposed to be like that but I decided to chow down anyway. The salmon was probably one of the best salmon I've ever had! Although I couldn't taste the honey mustard, the salmon was crispy enough and full of flavor. I highly suggest getting it. The salmon also came with veggies and potatoes. The potatoes didn't taste good at all. It lacked taste and texture. The veggies were kind of weird. Some were unidentifiable so I didn't know what I was eating. Also, the veggies came with fruits.

If you're a health junkie, I highly suggest trying this restaurant out.< /review>

< review>
Templeton Park is a great park for a kids play day or other get together event.

There's a large grilling and seating area with great summer shade. The park itself also has large trees throughout offing lots of large shady spots.

The weekly year round famers market held on Saturday 9am-12 is amongst the best in the country.

They also host a concert in the park series in the summer along with numerous other events year round.

For the water types you also have the summing pool. Which adds a great extra activity for family events held in the park.< /review>

< text>
Nice size park.  Decent playground and a lot of open grass areas and several nice tables with bbqs by some. Larger bbq for events. Fairly decent gazebo in center of park. Water fountains and bathrooms as well. Beautiful trees but with younger kids it's worth mentioning that there's not much in the way of fencing or borders from surrounding active streets.  And ants and wasps can be an issue in some parts of the year at this park. Great central location though also near highway,  food,  and gas. Templeton is beautiful if you've never seen it you ought to.< /text>

<Review>This park is a gem, and what I say is the heart and soul of Templeton. It's walking distance from just about everything in the historical part of downtown Templeton. This park is ALWAYS clean, and has more BBQ's than you can imagine. I really enjoy attending Templeton Park in the summer time for their "Concerts in the Park" series, and for the fourth of July festivities (includes parade, and doing your own fireworks). Great FREE concerts all summer long. Get there early for most events, because they fill up quick, and get very crowded, with a great and polite atmosphere.

< Review>
Great service, but a word of caution for holiday shoppers. Although UPS insures packages up to $50,000 in value, this store will not insure above the default $100 value unless they wrap the items themselves. If you are shipping a non-fragile but high value item, you are much better off going to a UPS Center or the Postal Service and insuring for the full replacement cost.

This store works best for dropping off small non-fragile packages or if you have an item that needs careful wrapping as well as shipping.<//Review>

< review>
I have eaten at Central Kitchen at least 20 times (it's near USC inside The Lorenzo residential complex)... the food is really tasty and very reasonable.  The burgers are great and so are the teriyaki bowls, love the Kale salad, and I'm addicted to the Salmon-yum! The Veggie pizza has lots of fresh vegetables on it and lots of flavor.  Oh, I had a breakfast burrito that was to die for.  I don't live at Lorenzo but if I did I'd eat there every day - the service is really good and friendly too.

In addition to the food and the service, it is really a nice place to be -most of the seating is outdoors and covered, it overlooks a big grassy lawn, and fountains. They have a ton of big screen TVs which is great for watching a game - and they now have beer on draft!<//review>

Warning!

I am transferring this over from another review site where I used to be active..this is my own review.
